A FEW THINGS TO NOTE:

Begin slowly with short 15 to 20 minute sessions on lower heat settings. I
recommend *starting with the green lights*. These lower temperatures are
also great for longer sessions, such as napping or working at your desk.

   - Slowly work your way to the higher temperature. (gold lights)
   - Stay hydrated by drinking plenty of water before and after each
   session.
   - Never lay your head directly on the mat when the heat is on.

As you begin using your Biomat regularly, you will feel changes in your
body and energy. You might feel more energy than usual, or you may find
yourself feeling a little more tired. Don’t worry; this is completely
normal.

   - One reason for these changes is that Biomat encourages circulation and
   detoxification.
   - If you feel overwhelmed by the changes, lower the temperatures and use
   shorter times.
   - As your body releases all the toxins, your energy will balance, and
   you will begin to feel great.

If you have any questions, I'm only a phone call away.

I’d put more money in ETH for now, let the auto investing run. Maybe put
some into AVAX and LINK and maybe a small amount into SHIBA (leave at least
$1000 of buying power so the auto investments run)

On Coinbase, maybe put some into ARB, Polygon

I would also maybe have your stock broker/financial advisor put 2% of your
investment money into the BTC and ETH ETFs, and maybe 0.5% into HUT, MARA,
COIN, and MSTR

I do think BTC could drop back to 85k or so, but will likely be $150k at
least by end of 2026, maybe hitting 200k+ at some point (which is about 2x
from current price), and likely solidly above $500k by 2030. It’s already
done 4-5x+ from the low this cycle since 2021.

ETH has lagged Bitcoin this cycle, but is 10x smaller. In a lot of ways
it’s more useful, but it has a lot of competition. It did probably 5x more
return than Bitcoin, and probably will do at least 2x better by the end of
this cycle (and is currently doing 2x+ worse, so likely will do 4x better
than Bitcoin from here). In prices, ETH is about 4k right now, and I think
10k is a safe bet by end of this year, if not sooner, and if not more like
15-20k.

All to say, I’m still holding and even buying more on days prices drop a
lot. If something spikes more than 25% in a day, I usually sell 10% of it
so, and try and buy back in if it drops, or just use that to fund the
recurring auto buys

*Transportation of Hazardous Materials*
Federal law forbids the carriage of hazardous materials aboard aircraft in
your luggage or on your person. A violation can result in civil penalties.
Examples include: Paints, aerosols, lighter fluid, fireworks, torch
lighters, tear gases and compressed gas cartridges.

There are special exceptions for small quantities (up to 70 ounces total).

*ADVICE TO INTERNATIONAL PASSENGERS ON LIMITATIONS OF LIABILITY*

Passengers embarking upon a journey involving an ultimate destination or a
stop in a country other than the country of departure are advised that the
provisions of an international treaty (the Warsaw Convention, the 1999
Montreal Convention, or other treaty), as well as a carrier’s own contract
of carriage or tariff provisions, may be applicable to their entire
journey, including any portion entirely within the countries of departure
and destination. The applicable treaty governs and may limit the liability
of carriers to passengers for death or personal injury, destruction or loss
of, or damage to, baggage, and for delay of passengers and baggage.

Additional protection can usually be obtained by purchasing insurance from
a private company. Such insurance is not affected by any limitation of the
carrier’s liability under an international treaty. For further information
please consult your airline or insurance company representative.

---------- Forwarded message ---------
From: Nektarios Liolios <nektarios@radish.credit>
Date: Mon, Oct 14, 2024 at 04:20
Subject: A Difficult Announcement Regarding Radish
To: Matthew Eisner <matteisn@gmail.com>
CC: Drew Graham <drew@radish.credit>, Vicky Zuiderent <vicky@radish.credit>,
Matej Ftacnik <matej@radish.credit>


Dear Matthew,

This is a message I was hoping to never have to write: despite our best
efforts and dedication, we have reached the conclusion that we are no
longer able to continue operations, and the company will be dissolved.
The new leadership and investment in early 2024 gave us hope and the
ability to progress faster but some essential funding we thought confirmed
fell through recently and left us over-exposed with no other option than to
stop.

We entered this journey full of optimism and determination, and I want to
sincerely thank you for the trust, support, and belief you placed in our
vision. Your investment allowed us to pursue something we were deeply
passionate about, and for that, we will always be grateful.

Unfortunately, the challenges we faced proved insurmountable, and despite
exploring various options, we were unable to achieve the success we had
hoped for. We recognise the responsibility we carried in managing your
investment, and I deeply regret that we were not able to deliver the return
you deserve.

Please accept my sincerest apologies for this outcome. While this chapter
is closing, I want you to know how much your partnership has meant to us,
and I hope we can stay connected for any future opportunities.
It saddens us that we did not manage to make the dream of fair financing
for underserved communities a reality. Time will tell if there is space for
a re-incarnated Radish in the future - we are certainly keen to stay in
touch.

We have initiated the process of striking off the company and are working
on making this as frictionless as possible. The only thing you should
expect from us is a letter informing you about the dissolution.

Happy to get on a call to answer any questions.

Thank you once again for everything.

Nektarios, Drew, Vicky & Matej

Intro bio may pigeon hole you out of some roles, but seems appropriate for
what you’re looking for.


Put skills above certifications


Use same casing for skills (see Design Thinking - I’d use all title case)


Any other thought leadership (or broaden to portfolio samples) you can
include in that section?





Backyard:

-Developed and implemented go-to-market strategies for 30+ product launches,

leading cross-functional teams and driving up to $6.5M in sales per launch

-Can you make this more: “Conducted in-depth consumer and competitive
research to identify buyer

personas and formalized brand and product identy, improving performance
across the brands by XX%”?

-Directed content strategy and copywriting,

optimizing conversion rates for 5 brands and resulting in a 15% average
increase in sales.

-Managed retention marketing for 200,000 contacts, including managing CRM
migration, email campaigns, automation, and reporting across 4 business
units, improving repeat sales by 20%.

-For the last bullet, I’d split into 1 point about influencer marketing,
and then use the metrics from the other points and maybe blend them into
point 2 and 4?



Skidmore

-Conducted in-depth research and analysis to develop strategy, messaging,
websites, email, and other creative for diverse clients in the CPG
industry, including packaged food and beverage brands such as …..

-Collaborated with cross-functional teams to create brand identity and
improve market positioning through audience definition, messaging
guidelines, and holistic brand experiences. (Examples, brands, campaign
reach or budget could all be good metrics here)

-Led website development projects from discovery to launch, ensuring
alignment with client objectives to deliver cohesive digital experiences on
time and under budget.

-I would work point 4 into the other 3


Akervall

-Any metrics, partner name drops, channel reach, marketing budgets, etc you
could pepper in here would be good

They have also delayed the process on their side in terms of delays of
providing details on improvement and rental income. I certainly harbor a
great deal of frustration for how this process has played out, and it has
cost me thousands of dollars in changing plans (and future revenue based on
the renewal being at way below market rate - so I regret my last
accomodation made for them at this point which was rushed due to their
pressuring), and a lot of time spent that I do not have to spare - not to
mention the stress and additional work caused by these continued hold up
tactics.

From talking to Will, it sounds like this will be finalized tomorrow when
the title responds to him to make sure another lien has not been taken on
the property. It sounds like signing this now is a significant risk until
that is confirmed. I'm okay to sign this tomorrow, but am not willing to
expose myself to the full liability of losing the house and escrow. I would
rather walk.

We can close on the 5th, but I will not be in town and am now very wary of
doing a full changing of locks/etc when this closes... not sure how
concerned I should be.

It sounds at this point, my hands are somewhat tied and that this is
somehow on me, which is a very uncomfortable situation.

somehow on me, which is a very uncomfortable situation.

potentially.


A little update - we now have 40+ assets on 4+ chains, and have grown from
800k TVL to more than $5m TVL in the last week alone. US company, SEC
transfer agent, on chain ERC-20s composable in DeFi, 3 founders who
previously founded 3 unicorns (Crunchyroll, LegalZoom, and Freenome), etc.
We also launched our B2B2C API to let tradfi/fintechs embed our assets in
their trading, savings, salary, exchange, and other apps to reach web2
users (in the hundreds of thousands now, millions by next month).

But we realized there is chicken-and-egg problem in RWAs of compliance and
liquidity (not to mention distribution), so we're spinning out a KYC'ed
DeFi platform, SolidViolet, which includes primary and secondary
liquidity aggregation, compliance controls for issuers, grants for issuers
in our native token, perps, and list on our B2B2C API.

Rough deck here:
https://docs.google.com/presentation/d/19KsytsY2Whs_KGGEdH6gdXztuOQZqyaygjvrxLabTCw/edit#slide=id.g2e76bc6011a_1_1

We opened up our private sale late over the weekend, and the first tranche
is basically already filled by a few big ticket investors (WAGMI, likely
GCR and 3-4 more - and commitments coming in for the second tranche as
well, including from Susquehanna SIG). We're signed to be the the
"preferred" DEX of Plume Network, and already have 10+ RWA issuers signed
up including Franklin Templeton, and pretty much every one we talk to is
super eager.

I've been scrambling to bring on some angels and other fast moving/small
funds to align some more people around us as we plan launch, so wanted to
reach out. I also imagine some of what you're building could be
complementary here, so would love to explore that.

A little update - we now have 40+ assets on 4+ chains, and have grown from
800k TVL to more than $5m TVL in the last week alone. US company, SEC
transfer agent, on chain ERC-20s composable in DeFi, 3 founders who
previously founded 3 unicorns (Crunchyroll, LegalZoom, and Freenome), etc.
We also launched our B2B2C API to let tradfi/fintechs embed our assets in
their trading, savings, salary, exchange, and other apps to reach web2
users (in the hundreds of thousands now, millions by next month).

But we realized there is chicken-and-egg problem in RWAs of compliance and
liquidity (not to mention distribution), so we're spinning out a KYC'ed
DeFi platform, SolidViolet, which includes primary and secondary
liquidity aggregation, compliance controls for issuers, grants for issuers
in our native token, perps, and list on our B2B2C API.

Rough deck here:
https://docs.google.com/presentation/d/19KsytsY2Whs_KGGEdH6gdXztuOQZqyaygjvrxLabTCw/edit#slide=id.g2e76bc6011a_1_1

We opened up our private sale late over the weekend, and already almost
have the first tranche filled by a few big ticket investors (WAGMI, likely
GCR and 3-4 more - and we have commitments coming in for the second tranche
as well, including from Susquehanna SIG). We're signed to be the the
"preferred" DEX of Plume Network, and already have 10+ RWA issuers signed
up, and pretty much every one we talk to super eager.

I've been scrambling to bring on some angels and other fast moving/small

Hi Gabe,

I wanted to proactively raise that it is unlikely I reach our goal of $5m
raised by the end of this week. $1m is likely, $2m is not unreasonable, and
$3m is feasible if all goes well. But these may be SAFT signings, not
checks in.

I do think we have a clearer path to $5m than we did a month ago, and that
would probably be pretty doable by the end of July. Additionally, it seems
like there are a number of other streams that could potentially break in
the coming weeks (B2B targeted marketing, partner case studies, email
launch, etc).

However, I am aware that I have not achieved our target, and that that is a
significant shortcoming. I am continuing to go full speed ahead with
outreach, but am realizing that may not be ideal for the company depending
on what your plan is. To that end, I am wondering how you want me to
proceed - whether planning for my departure in a way that is as smooth as
possible as that is what you had said before, or taking a bit more time to
follow up on these conversations/finding a path forward that makes sense
and continuing to move full speed ahead.

I do very much believe in what we are building, enjoy working with our
team, and am very excited by where we are going. This has been a tricky
time for me which should be ending Friday with the close of my house.
However, that is certainly not an excuse for not achieving our goals.

Let me know your thoughts,

Matthew

date: 2024-06-21
to: amit@borderlesscapital.io
subject: Dinari update and SVLT private sale round 1 closing
msg_id: 190396d4ea41e144
---

Hi,

Hope all is well!

I wanted to make a point to send you an update to see if I might be able to
get you involved with what we're doing at Dinari/SolidViolet, as I've seen
how Borderless has grown since the Algorand Accelerator days :)

On the Dinari side:

   - We're up to 40+ 1:1 backed tokenized assets on 3 chains (with Kinto
   and Base launching in the next weeks). GME got a great reception when we
   launched a few weeks ago, and 24 hour trading on Camelot for that has been
   a hit


   - We've nearly 2x'ed our TVL in the past month, and have a couple of
   large blockchain grants that we're onboarding in the coming days that will
   bring us deep into 7 figures (and we finally have proper data feeds for all
   our tokens on DeFillama :) )


   - The majority of our growth and volume has come from our B2B2C APIs,
   which enable developers, web2 FinTechs, web3 projects, and enterprises to
   integrate ours (and soon via SolidViolet, other RWA issuers') assets into
   their app with 2 lines of code. We now reach nearly 300k+ investors through
   10 B2B2C partners, all of which have launched in the last month, and we
   have 20+ more onboarding before end of July


On the SolidViolet side:

   - Token Sale: we're in the midst of the private sale (more details
   below), and will ramp up to a public sale/protocol launch/token
   listing/likely airdrops in early Fall


   - Issuers Partners: we've onboarded about 10 RWA issuer partners, and
   have about 30 more who want to. Pretty much everyone we talk to is very
   keen to have compliant/KYC'ed defi, aggregated liquidity across primary and
   secondary markets, and distribution via our B2B2C API partners


   - Plume + other partners: we've signed an agreement to be the
   "preferred" DEX for Plume Network, and have a number of similar deals
   coming together.


Currently, I just opened earlier this week (and am now closing out the
first tranches of our private token sale (which has been quite a floodgate
since we opened it a few days ago).

We're likely closing the first tranche next week, and the second the
following. We've had a few big ticket investors that have confirmed and are
weighing check size (and we're figuring out how we'll spread their
allocation across the tranches). I'd love to try and get in more strategic
investors while we can squeeze them in before they close (definitely start
of next week, possibly through next Friday) or for the second tranche.

If you might be interested (even a very small ticket), or might know people
who would be or could help in meaningful ways, would love to chat - i'd be
happy to give you advisor allocation for a few intros. And generally would
love to have you on board if possible!

I've included a deck here that includes token allocation, sale pricing, and
some other info - feel free to share 1:1, but we aren't circulating
publicly yet:
https://docs.google.com/presentation/d/19KsytsY2Whs_KGGEdH6gdXztuOQZqyaygjvrxLabTCw/edit#slide=id.g2e734a40a9b_0_1025


Let me know if any of that might be of interest, or happy to answer any
questions you have/jump on a call.

Best,

Matthew

---

   integrate ours (and soon via SolidViolet, other RWA issuers') assets into
   their app with 2 lines of code. We now reach nearly 300k+ investors through

   have 20+ more onboarding before end of July

   listing/likely airdrops in early Fall

We appear to be nearing a resolution on this transaction, yet we've been at

financial impact on the seller - by way of loss rent for the garden level
unit. I am working diligently to keep the deal together and am asking for
your assistance to get us back under contract.

It's important that we acknowledge the seller's position: a default
occurred at the end of May, granting the seller rightful claim to the EMD.
To facilitate moving forward, the seller has generously agreed to extend
the contract by an additional two weeks, effectively granting a month's
extension in total. In return, the seller simply asks the buyer to
acknowledge that the EMD belongs to the seller in case the deal doesn't
close.

Up until now, the seller has made concessions without receiving anything in
exchange. To get this deal back on track, I kindly request that the buyer
sign the attached addendum promptly.

I also want you to know that the upper floor tenants want to renew their
lease for another year at the rate of $2,600/MO. The seller doesn't want to
risk losing the tenants if the transaction doesn't close and intends to
renew the lease.

Hi Amy,

I have changed lenders, and have some slightly different requirement for
the insurance to close. Can you provide the following for 4727 Trumbull:

RE: insurance we’ll need to see the Insurance binder and invoice OR paid
receipt. The insurance policy needs the following:

   - Insurance policy needs to be under the business name, *Vang Advisory
   LLC*
   - Policy needs:
   -
      - Rent Loss Coverage for 6 months
      - Dwelling Coverage of $466,000 or greater
      - Liability Insurance of 100k minimum
   - Policy needs to designate a Mortgagee Clause for the following:
   -
      - Fay Servicing LLC
      ISAOA/ ATIMA
      PO Box 7047
      Troy, MI 48007-7047


Please cc will on any communication around this to expedite process.

Best,

Matthew

date: 2024-05-14
to: Sierra S <ssoleima92@gmail.com>
subject: Re: Resume
msg_id: 18f75bd39c648728
---

CV feedback:

-formatting is wonky in Google Docs/Pages. I’m sure fine in word, but
Gdocs/Dropbox allow you to update files, and PDF ensures formatting

-ATS friendly CV vs human-read CV - I used LinkedIn for ATS, you could even
use website for human read

-Action oriented job detail points - I use a format of “[VERBED]
[TASK/WORKSTREAM/RESPONIBILITY] to
[IMPOVEMENT/ACCOMPLISHMENT/METRIC/OUTPUT/PARTNERS] - happy to help you
iterate this if you take a stab - no more than 5 per job and focusing on
most important/relevant

-Generalize tools/etc in job description bullets and group into skills
section - consider adding more space for this via columns/etc in human read
version (ideally 1 page, okay if ATS version is 2)


Cover Letter:

-create one, then ask ChatGPT to create versions of it to fit a few types
of jobs/companies - easy way to stand out in 1-click apply applications

Sites to use: Wellfound, Remotejobs, Unicornhunt (I’d look to remote job
boards particularly, and LinkedIn easy apply)


Questions:

-Would you want to transition out of your current job by taking on a part
time contract/shorter term project (and looking for another job or more
contracts on the side)?

-What do you want to get better at or focus on in your next job? What
tasks/jobs do you NOT want to do? Any other excluding ciretria apart from
remote?

-What are your weaknesses? Strengths?

-What are your stories you tell about your career path? How you operate in
a work environment? Etc?

-happy to send you my CV if that’s helpful haha - it’s a bit dated. Or some
of the ones I shortlisted when I was hiring for a marketing manager
recently


Everything here is pretty easy - we can knock it out in an hour or two -
you may not even need to realistically, but hiring processes are all about
looking for a reason to eliminate candidates


All to say this is quite a good place to be 😚

---------- Forwarded message ---------
From: Pawel Tomczuk - TechTree <pawel@techtree.dev>
Date: Fri, May 10, 2024 at 00:48
Subject: 👾 TechTree - April update
To: <matteisn@gmail.com>


Our research agent use case that helped us to get 100k USD revenue in Q1 -
how we combine LLM-powered AI with hedge-fund like decision-making engine
*Dear investors and friends,*
*TechTree - who we are & what we do*

TechTree enables organizations to combine their personal & organization
networks and their prospects in one space [their private “LinkedIn
instance”] and deploy agents combining LLM-powered language & context
skills with a hedge fund-like approach [powered by unique data set
combining Linkedin & Crunchbase data on a person level] to the selection
process.

We want to help professionals spend less time on routine tasks that robots
do better than humans. [finding entities with specific criteria & outreach
to them]. Our initial focus is the venture-backed space.

*TLDR APRIL: sharing results of combining our data with an automated
agent-led outreach experiment*

   1. One of the areas we think a lot about disrupting is the work done by
   mostly junior people that can fit the following flow:
   a) Access a database (LinkedIn Recruiter / Sales Nav, Crunchbase, Apollo
   etc.)
   b) Find entities meeting certain criteria (people, companies etc.)
   c) Reach out with a templated message
   d) Hand over to a more senior person when someone comes back with
   interest.

   This flow is seen in multiple places, but we have narrowed it down to 3
   areas:
   - specialized recruitment
   - outbound sales for enterprise products
   - VC investing

   *Our goal is to combine the LLM-powered agents & automation with a hedge
   fund-like data platform that makes it possible to select the right entities
   for the reach out.*

   2. Since Q4 last year, we have been experimenting with using the data we
   have on our platform to automate one of the flows above - given our domain
   knowledge we focused on "specialized recruitment".

   3. After testing the approach internally we got introduced to a few
   clients looking for key engineering hires who engaged us for a success fee.
   We used a fully automated approach to fulfill that:

   4. *Results:*
   - over 5000 candidates analysed
   - over 500 outreach messages sent
   - over 60 candidates introduced to clients
   - over 88% of candidates invited for the interview
   - 9 candidates hired (and over 100k USD in revenue generated)

Here's a bit more insight from the recent post in our product newsletter
<https://mytechtree.us4.list-manage.com/track/click?u=4135e2ef2145fe862c7d0c864&id=797f96d2d6&e=4464ef8ea9>

*Our conclusion:*
Combining LLMs and Gen AI-powered agents with a hedge fund-like
decision-making engine is a combination that can deliver great outcomes
even for a very demanding client.
*📈 Traction (commercial update)*

*Overview:* We're sharing more about the step-by-step approach our
agent-led outreach approach below. We're now trying to onboard some "alpha
users" for our talent research agent offering [see more below]

At the same time, we're onboarding some alpha users for our dashboard
focusing on 3 areas:

   1. Network management & co-pilot for VC & PE firms

   2. Research agent increasing efficiency of research function for
   executive search & recruitment firms [here's more about our "research
   agent" offering
   <https://mytechtree.us4.list-manage.com/track/click?u=4135e2ef2145fe862c7d0c864&id=6345050631&e=4464ef8ea9>
   ]

   3. Connections strength data finding the best intro path to potential
   clients via our "connection strength" feature


*Details of our automated agent-led outreach approach:*

   1. We automatically created LinkedIn searches based on job descriptions
   from companies and import 200-800 results per project to TechTree *[Long
   list]*
   2. We’re enriching data via our platform to get all LinkedIn info,
   connected with CrunchBase, Dealroom etc. on a person level *[enrichment]*
   3. We’re using TechTree score* [career quality score]* & experience by
   stage to narrow the list to 20-50 people *[shortlist]*
   4. We use AI on top of our data to create personalized outreach messages
   and automatically send them via Linkedin *[personalized outreach]*
   5. We connect interested candidates to hiring managers

What was particularly important for us was the quality of companies and the
importance of the roles and profiles that we have helped them to
attract. This approach has led to 9 hires (with 6 of them being AI / ML
engineers) in Q1’24 including the likes:

   - Open AI-backed AI book-keeping agent
   - hired Staff Engineer (15+years of experience, ex-Nvidia and Meta, with
   founder experience)
   - EarlyBird-backed AI agent building apps on top of dev documentation
   - hired Machine Learning Engineer (15+years of experience, technical
   founder with a successful exit to unicorn fintech)
   - Daniel Gross & Nat Friedmann backed general purpose AI agent founded
   by Llama-2 co-author,
   - hired Senior Backend Engineer (15+years of experience, was the 1st
   employee at a unicorn SaaS who stayed there for over 7 years)

Some other stats worth mentioning:

   - 88% of candidates presented to clients were invited for interviews by
   clients
   - 77% of processes took less than 3 weeks from the start to accept the
   offer.

Other clients who hired through us included a top 5 VC fund in Europe (Full
Stack Engineer), an enterprise blockchain scale-up (2 engineers - 1 role
was open for over 6 months), a top PE-backed payments business and a few
more.

*Based on the result of this experiment we're continuing with the following
actions:*

   - Experimenting with personalized outreach
   - Building our own Chrome extension to remove reliance on 3rd party tools
   - Test "research agent" offering with a focus on recruitment companies -
   instead of hiring junior staff like researchers & associates, they can use
   TT to find relevant candidates for the research

*Other development*

   1. Negotiation of POC terms with one of the biggest global consulting
   companies
   2. Successful completion of a pilot for Series A VC fund & discussions
   about the scope of potential long-term cooperation (approx. 4-6x budget of
   POC)
   3. Onboarded 5 test users for the freemium version
   4. Discussing partnership for AI-agent-led recruitment with one of the
   top European VCs in the AI space (investor of 2 companies who already hired
   people via our agent-led solution)

*🔧 Product update*

*Overview:* We've added some cool features that can help our users to
better manage their network & create value thanks to it. Here's a loom
video covering the latest updates.
<https://mytechtree.us4.list-manage.com/track/click?u=4135e2ef2145fe862c7d0c864&id=3254c74b5b&e=4464ef8ea9>

   1. AI summary & chat - *what's unique about our approach:*
   *because our DB is structured (i.e. not a block of text, but tabular
   data with the same structure for every entity) you can manage context
   - select "categories of information" that are included in the summary
   *you can create the summary for multiple people/companies and use
   prompts to iterate it (for example compare)
   *you can use prompts in the "summary chat" to create outreach messages,
   forwardable intros and more

   2. Connection strength - see who from your network is the best
   connection to the prospect
   *We enable users to create a prospects list
   *they can see how people from their network (for example employees of
   their company or 1st degree connections from LinkedIn) are connected to
   that person
   *our score is based on shared work history taking into account things
   like tenure, seniority of both people at the time of working together, size
   of the company, country, location etc.

   3. UX / UI improvements:
   *Better network management - users can add people to multiple lists at
   the same time
   *Resume view of a person including all professional details

Also, we have updated our data documentation
<https://mytechtree.us4.list-manage.com/track/click?u=4135e2ef2145fe862c7d0c864&id=8462b50ff5&e=4464ef8ea9>
-
if you'd like to power your applications / data models with a unique set of
people / company data, please get in touch.

Hi Regan,

Hope all is well since we spoke some years back when you were first setting
up Lattice. I've been running the GTM at Dinari for about 8 months now, and
was curious if you might have any advice from us, or more of a moonshot, if
you might introduce us to someone at CoinList.

We issue 1:1 backed compliant tokenized stocks/ETFs, currently 40 on 3
chains, founded by founders of Crunchyroll, LegalZoom, and a 10bn cancer
screening ai biotech firm, 10m seed from Balaji/500/SIG/etc.

A good analogy is Circle for equities, but with an additional B2B2C SaaS
model enabling emerging market fintechs to create solutions such as
"Robinhood for Argentina" with a stripe style API (we have about 5 of these
partners live with another 20 or so launching) and are planning to spin out
a compliant RWA DEX and token with sale.

We're rounding up our first batch of early partners for our launch
announcement in May (it looks like we're already slated to be Plume
Network's official DEX), so would love any tips you have for us as we go
into solidifying the plans for our token sale.

Happy to send along some more info or would love to find some time to chat.

Best,

Matthew

date: 2024-03-29
to: Sophie Donkin <sophie.donkin@gmail.com>
subject: Re: Catching up
msg_id: 18e885cf4ba5e497
---

Okay, following up with promised info:

Dinari, Inc. is a Delaware C Corporation. We have raised approximately $10MM
from seed financing. Dinari, Inc. has only one director: Gabe Otte, our CEO.
Dinari, Inc., has a wholly-owned subsidiary, Dinari Holdings LLC (a DE LLC). 
It's  purpose is a buffer between Dinari  and our eventual dealings as broker
dealer. That subsidiary has a wholly-owned subsidiary, Dinari Securities, LLC
(also a DE LLC). That subsidiary is the entity applying for the broker dealer
license. We will likely form our Bermuda subsidiary for our token/spin
our protocol from Dinari, Inc., or the Holding Company - that is still TBD.
Dinari, Inc. is a registered Transfer Agent with the SEC. We are currently not
actively engaged in any active transfer agent duties.
Most of the procedures that we have for risk are managed through our external
vendors for KYC/KYB and AML. Once we have a broker dealer, we will have a new
set of procedures for BD risk
Here's an additional legal FAQ doc that may be useful:
https://docs.google.com/document/d/1fIqfZfVzlT1geOHnzbL_csoPu3jo4cV4S4hNLoWNKTc/edit


Answering your partnership questions: * How formal an agreement are you looking
   for? MOI/LOI or something more structured? Initially very loose MOU most
   likely so we can secure some early partners, but ideally tightening up as
   much as possible over time to ensure our partners actually integrate with us
   or otherwise deliver on the partnership. Sounds like one of my next
   priorities should be to more thoroughly map the types of partners and what we
   would expect from them.

 * Are any funds/tokens being paid by you to the partners or vice versa? We
   would be giving them tokens or committing liquidity to their RWA assets in
   our DEX to incentive them integrating (and for other services or support
   other types of partners would provide)

 * What services are the partners providing and what services are you
   providing?Core partners will be RWA issuers who's  assets would be on our
   marketplace. We'd also likely be looking for blockchains to provide grants,
   other blockchain infra to provide services, marketing/pr agency partners,
   market makers (which we have an offer from FalconX I'd be curious your take
   on that I've attached), DeFi protocols, FinTech apps that will use our
   assets, and really anyone we can line up.

 * What risk are you taking by relying on these partners?We are somewhat relying
   on them to be stable and compliant. However, we will operate a permissioned
   model, so if we find they are not living up to standards of engagement or
   compliance, we would have a mechanism to delist them, at which point the cost
   becomes the tokens (which I imagine we would lockup conditionally) and
   opportunity cost of focusing on other partners

date: 2024-03-18
to: Guillaume Agis <guillaume.agis@gmail.com>
subject: Re: Tezos accelerator
msg_id: 18e53598b965347b
---

Our core product is an obfuscated API to allow developers and businesses
(or smart contracts for web3) to embed stocks into their products without
the compliance lift of local banking or brokerage licenses (and we leverage
them to bring our products to local markets), or with benefits of defi
yield. We have about 10 partners that have just launched or are launching
in the next month, and probably another 50 in pipeline.

We also have general defi use cases, but these are more degens and crypto
whales, but there’s some sexy yield there were productizing for more mass
market investors.

Almost nobody is doing anything like this in the US, they’re too scared -
and everyone outside the US working on this are just pump and dumping
tokens, which the SEC is not down with and they oversee the underlying
assets, so that’s not sustainible. but our CLO was GC at legalzoom for 15
years, and Freenome was very much a regulatory/compliance play, and we took
the most compliant/long term approach possible, so it’s playing out well.
But real meaningful traction for “RWAs” is probably a couple years off.
Also our developeds founded/built crunchyroll. And we actually don’t allow
us users to mint/burn for compliance reasons

It’s basically like a real version of Mirror protocol if you remember those.

Let me know if you start doing more BD/IR, happy to make some connections.

Hi Nektarios,

Hope you're well since we last spoke!

I wanted to reach out as I'm working on something I think you might find
interesting, and might be able to help me a bit with :)

We (dinari.com) tokenize stocks with 1:1 backing and dividend payouts in a super
compliant manner (SEC transfer agent license, US company, no native governance
or protocol token - basically Circle for Equities) - currently 30+ assets on
Arbitrum, with Etherum launching next month.

We're found some early traction working with FinTech's in emerging markets that
are working on solutions like decentralized/localized Robinhoods,
payments/remittance apps, wealth managers, we'd love to find a
Neobank/challenger bank, etc. that use our smart contracts or APIs to embed
equities in their products with essentially no compliance lift related to US
equities.

Would you be up to jump on a call sometime? I'd love to hear your stream of
consciousness thoughts, as I imagine you'd help guide us in some helpful
directions. And would love to hear about how Radish is coming!

Let me know if there might be some times that work for you,

Matthew

to select "Estimated Tax" as reason  for 2023  tax year is no longer possible.

Payment info below:
For the IRS payments of $3,650, pay on January 15th
https://www.irs.gov/payments/direct-pay
Make a Payment
Reason: Estimated Tax
Apply to:  1040ES
Tax Period: 2023
Tax Year for Verification: 2021
Filing Status: Single
Use your California address, as that is what was listed on your 2021 return.

Matthew
